<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.AccountImmutabilityPolicyProperties">AccountImmutabilityPolicyProperties
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ImmutableStorageAccount">ImmutableStorageAccount</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>This defines account-level immutability policy properties.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowProtectedAppendWrites</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowProtectedAppendWrites: This property can only be changed for disabled and unlocked time-based retention policies.
When enabled, new blocks can be written to an append blob while maintaining immutability protection and compliance. Only
new blocks can be added and any existing blocks cannot be modified or deleted.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>immutabilityPeriodSinceCreationInDays</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ImmutabilityPeriodSinceCreationInDays: The immutability period for the blobs in the container since the policy creation,
in days.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>state</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.AccountImmutabilityPolicyProperties_State">
AccountImmutabilityPolicyProperties_State
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>State: The ImmutabilityPolicy state defines the mode of the policy. Disabled state disables the policy, Unlocked state
allows increase and decrease of immutability retention time and also allows toggling allowProtectedAppendWrites
property, Locked state only allows the increase of the immutability retention time. A policy can only be created in a
Disabled or Unlocked state and can be toggled between the two states. Only a policy in an Unlocked state can transition
to a Locked state which cannot be reverted.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ChangeFeed">ChangeFeed
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccounts_BlobService_Spec">StorageAccounts_BlobService_Spec</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>The blob service properties for change feed events.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>enabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Enabled: Indicates whether change feed event logging is enabled for the Blob service.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>retentionInDays</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>RetentionInDays: Indicates the duration of changeFeed retention in days. Minimum value is 1 day and maximum value is
146000 days (400 years). A null value indicates an infinite retention of the change feed.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>enabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Enabled: Indicates whether change feed event logging is enabled for the Blob service.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>retentionInDays</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>RetentionInDays: Indicates the duration of changeFeed retention in days. Minimum value is 1 day and maximum value is
146000 days (400 years). A null value indicates an infinite retention of the change feed.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.CorsRule">CorsRule
</h3>

<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>

<em>
[]string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowedHeaders: Required if CorsRule element is present. A list of headers allowed to be part of the cross-origin
request.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowedMethods</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.CorsRule_AllowedMethods">
[]CorsRule_AllowedMethods
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowedMethods: Required if CorsRule element is present. A list of HTTP methods that are allowed to be executed by the
origin.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowedOrigins</code><br/>
<em>
[]string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowedOrigins: Required if CorsRule element is present. A list of origin domains that will be allowed via CORS, or &ldquo;*&rdquo;
to allow all domains</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>exposedHeaders</code><br/>
<em>
[]string
</em>
</td>

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>maxAgeInSeconds</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>MaxAgeInSeconds: Required if CorsRule element is present. The number of seconds that the client/browser should cache a
preflight response.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<p>ExposedHeaders: Required if CorsRule element is present. A list of response headers to expose to CORS clients.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>maxAgeInSeconds</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>MaxAgeInSeconds: Required if CorsRule element is present. The number of seconds that the client/browser should cache a
preflight response.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.DeleteRetentionPolicy">DeleteRetentionPolicy
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccounts_BlobService_Spec">StorageAccounts_BlobService_Spec</a>, <a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccounts_FileService_Spec">StorageAccounts_FileService_Spec</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>The service properties for soft delete.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowPermanentDelete</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowPermanentDelete: This property when set to true allows deletion of the soft deleted blob versions and snapshots.
This property cannot be used blob restore policy. This property only applies to blob service and does not apply to
containers or file share.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>days</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Days: Indicates the number of days that the deleted item should be retained. The minimum specified value can be 1 and
the maximum value can be 365.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>

</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AccessTier: Access tier for specific share. GpV2 account can choose between TransactionOptimized (default), Hot, and
Cool. FileStorage account can choose Premium.</p>

<td>

share.</p>

<td>
<code>metadata</code><br/>
<em>
map[string]string
</em>
</td>

</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>RootSquash: The property is for NFS share only. The default is NoRootSquash.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>shareQuota</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ShareQuota: The maximum size of the share, in gigabytes. Must be greater than 0, and less than or equal to 5TB (5120).
For Large File Shares, the maximum size is 102400.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.GeoReplicationStats_STATUS">GeoReplicationStats_STATUS
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccount_STATUS">StorageAccount_STATUS</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Statistics related to replication for storage account&rsquo;s Blob, Table, Queue and File services. It is only available when
geo-redundant replication is enabled for the storage account.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>canFailover</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CanFailover: A boolean flag which indicates whether or not account failover is supported for the account.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>lastSyncTime</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>LastSyncTime: All primary writes preceding this UTC date/time value are guaranteed to be available for read operations.
Primary writes following this point in time may or may not be available for reads. Element may be default value if value
of LastSyncTime is not available, this can happen if secondary is offline or we are in bootstrap.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>status</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.GeoReplicationStats_Status_STATUS">
GeoReplicationStats_Status_STATUS
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Status: The status of the secondary location. Possible values are: - Live: Indicates that the secondary location is
active and operational. - Bootstrap: Indicates initial synchronization from the primary location to the secondary
location is in progress.This typically occurs when replication is first enabled. - Unavailable: Indicates that the
secondary location is temporarily unavailable.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ImmutabilityPolicyProperties_STATUS">ImmutabilityPolicyProperties_STATUS
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccounts_BlobServices_Container_STATUS">StorageAccounts_BlobServices_Container_STATUS</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>The properties of an ImmutabilityPolicy of a blob container.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowProtectedAppendWrites</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowProtectedAppendWrites: This property can only be changed for unlocked time-based retention policies. When enabled,
new blocks can be written to an append blob while maintaining immutability protection and compliance. Only new blocks
can be added and any existing blocks cannot be modified or deleted. This property cannot be changed with
ExtendImmutabilityPolicy API.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowProtectedAppendWritesAll</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowProtectedAppendWritesAll: This property can only be changed for unlocked time-based retention policies. When
enabled, new blocks can be written to both &lsquo;Append and Bock Blobs&rsquo; while maintaining immutability protection and
compliance. Only new blocks can be added and any existing blocks cannot be modified or deleted. This property cannot be
changed with ExtendImmutabilityPolicy API. The &lsquo;allowProtectedAppendWrites&rsquo; and &lsquo;allowProtectedAppendWritesAll&rsquo;
properties are mutually exclusive.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>etag</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Etag: ImmutabilityPolicy Etag.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>immutabilityPeriodSinceCreationInDays</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ImmutabilityPeriodSinceCreationInDays: The immutability period for the blobs in the container since the policy creation,
in days.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>state</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ImmutabilityPolicyProperty_State_STATUS">
ImmutabilityPolicyProperty_State_STATUS
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>State: The ImmutabilityPolicy state of a blob container, possible values include: Locked and Unlocked.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>updateHistory</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.UpdateHistoryProperty_STATUS">
[]UpdateHistoryProperty_STATUS
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>UpdateHistory: The ImmutabilityPolicy update history of the blob container.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ImmutableStorageAccount">ImmutableStorageAccount
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccount_Spec">StorageAccount_Spec</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>This property enables and defines account-level immutability. Enabling the feature auto-enables Blob Versioning.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>enabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Enabled: A boolean flag which enables account-level immutability. All the containers under such an account have
object-level immutability enabled by default.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>immutabilityPolicy</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.AccountImmutabilityPolicyProperties">
AccountImmutabilityPolicyProperties
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ImmutabilityPolicy: Specifies the default account-level immutability policy which is inherited and applied to objects
that do not possess an explicit immutability policy at the object level. The object-level immutability policy has higher
precedence than the container-level immutability policy, which has a higher precedence than the account-level
immutability policy.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ManagementPolicyFilter">ManagementPolicyFilter
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ManagementPolicyDefinition">ManagementPolicyDefinition</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Filters limit rule actions to a subset of blobs within the storage account. If multiple filters are defined, a logical
AND is performed on all filters.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>blobIndexMatch</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.TagFilter">
[]TagFilter
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>BlobIndexMatch: An array of blob index tag based filters, there can be at most 10 tag filters</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>blobTypes</code><br/>
<em>
[]string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>BlobTypes: An array of predefined enum values. Currently blockBlob supports all tiering and delete actions. Only delete
actions are supported for appendBlob.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>prefixMatch</code><br/>
<em>
[]string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>PrefixMatch: An array of strings for prefixes to be match.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

[]string

<p>RoutingChoice: Routing Choice defines the kind of network routing opted by the user.</p>
</td>
</tr>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.RoutingPreference_STATUS_ARM">RoutingPreference_STATUS_ARM

<p>

</p>

data, the default option is microsoft routing</p>

<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>

</td>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.SmbSetting">SmbSetting
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ProtocolSettings">ProtocolSettings</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Setting for SMB protocol</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>authenticationMethods</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AuthenticationMethods: SMB authentication methods supported by server. Valid values are NTLMv2, Kerberos. Should be
passed as a string with delimiter &lsquo;;&rsquo;.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>channelEncryption</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ChannelEncryption: SMB channel encryption supported by server. Valid values are AES-128-CCM, AES-128-GCM, AES-256-GCM.
Should be passed as a string with delimiter &lsquo;;&rsquo;.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>kerberosTicketEncryption</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>KerberosTicketEncryption: Kerberos ticket encryption supported by server. Valid values are RC4-HMAC, AES-256. Should be
passed as a string with delimiter &lsquo;;&rsquo;</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>multichannel</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.Multichannel">
Multichannel
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Multichannel: Multichannel setting. Applies to Premium FileStorage only.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>versions</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Versions: SMB protocol versions supported by server. Valid values are SMB2.1, SMB3.0, SMB3.1.1. Should be passed as a
string with delimiter &lsquo;;&rsquo;.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

</h3>

(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ProtocolSettings_STATUS">ProtocolSettings_STATUS</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Setting for SMB protocol</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>authenticationMethods</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AuthenticationMethods: SMB authentication methods supported by server. Valid values are NTLMv2, Kerberos. Should be
passed as a string with delimiter &lsquo;;&rsquo;.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>channelEncryption</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ChannelEncryption: SMB channel encryption supported by server. Valid values are AES-128-CCM, AES-128-GCM, AES-256-GCM.
Should be passed as a string with delimiter &lsquo;;&rsquo;.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>kerberosTicketEncryption</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>KerberosTicketEncryption: Kerberos ticket encryption supported by server. Valid values are RC4-HMAC, AES-256. Should be
passed as a string with delimiter &lsquo;;&rsquo;</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>multichannel</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.Multichannel_STATUS">
Multichannel_STATUS
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Multichannel: Multichannel setting. Applies to Premium FileStorage only.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>versions</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Versions: SMB protocol versions supported by server. Valid values are SMB2.1, SMB3.0, SMB3.1.1. Should be passed as a
string with delimiter &lsquo;;&rsquo;.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_ARM">StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_ARM
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccount_Spec_ARM">StorageAccount_Spec_ARM</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>The parameters used to create the storage account.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>accessTier</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_AccessTier">
StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_AccessTier
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AccessTier: Required for storage accounts where kind = BlobStorage. The access tier is used for billing. The &lsquo;Premium&rsquo;
access tier is the default value for premium block blobs storage account type and it cannot be changed for the premium
block blobs storage account type.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowBlobPublicAccess</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowBlobPublicAccess: Allow or disallow public access to all blobs or containers in the storage account. The default
interpretation is true for this property.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowCrossTenantReplication</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowCrossTenantReplication: Allow or disallow cross AAD tenant object replication. The default interpretation is true
for this property.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowSharedKeyAccess</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowSharedKeyAccess: Indicates whether the storage account permits requests to be authorized with the account access
key via Shared Key. If false, then all requests, including shared access signatures, must be authorized with Azure
Active Directory (Azure AD). The default value is null, which is equivalent to true.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowedCopyScope</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_AllowedCopyScope">
StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_AllowedCopyScope
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowedCopyScope: Restrict copy to and from Storage Accounts within an AAD tenant or with Private Links to the same VNet.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>azureFilesIdentityBasedAuthentication</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.AzureFilesIdentityBasedAuthentication_ARM">
AzureFilesIdentityBasedAuthentication_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AzureFilesIdentityBasedAuthentication: Provides the identity based authentication settings for Azure Files.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>customDomain</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.CustomDomain_ARM">
CustomDomain_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomDomain: User domain assigned to the storage account. Name is the CNAME source. Only one custom domain is supported
per storage account at this time. To clear the existing custom domain, use an empty string for the custom domain name
property.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>defaultToOAuthAuthentication</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>DefaultToOAuthAuthentication: A boolean flag which indicates whether the default authentication is OAuth or not. The
default interpretation is false for this property.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>dnsEndpointType</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_DnsEndpointType">
StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_DnsEndpointType
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>DnsEndpointType: Allows you to specify the type of endpoint. Set this to AzureDNSZone to create a large number of
accounts in a single subscription, which creates accounts in an Azure DNS Zone and the endpoint URL will have an
alphanumeric DNS Zone identifier.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>encryption</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.Encryption_ARM">
Encryption_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Encryption: Encryption settings to be used for server-side encryption for the storage account.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>immutableStorageWithVersioning</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ImmutableStorageAccount_ARM">
ImmutableStorageAccount_ARM
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ImmutableStorageWithVersioning: The property is immutable and can only be set to true at the account creation time. When
set to true, it enables object level immutability for all the new containers in the account by default.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isHnsEnabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>IsHnsEnabled: Account HierarchicalNamespace enabled if sets to true.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isLocalUserEnabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isNfsV3Enabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>isSftpEnabled</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>

</td>

<tr>
<td>

</em>
</td>

</td>

<tr>
<td>
<code>largeFileSharesState</code><br/>

<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_LargeFileSharesState">

</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>LargeFileSharesState: Allow large file shares if sets to Enabled. It cannot be disabled once it is enabled.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>minimumTlsVersion</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_MinimumTlsVersion">

</a>
</em>
</td>

1.0 for this property.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>

</td>

</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>PublicNetworkAccess: Allow or disallow public network access to Storage Account. Value is optional but if passed in,
must be &lsquo;Enabled&rsquo; or &lsquo;Disabled&rsquo;.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>

</a>
</em>

</a>
</em>
</td>

</td>
</tr>

</em>
</td>

StorageAccountProperties_AccessTier_STATUS
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AccessTier: Required for storage accounts where kind = BlobStorage. The access tier is used for billing. The &lsquo;Premium&rsquo;
access tier is the default value for premium block blobs storage account type and it cannot be changed for the premium
block blobs storage account type.</p>

interpretation is true for this property.</p>

<td>
<code>allowCrossTenantReplication</code><br/>

bool

<code>allowSharedKeyAccess</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>

<p>AllowSharedKeyAccess: Indicates whether the storage account permits requests to be authorized with the account access
key via Shared Key. If false, then all requests, including shared access signatures, must be authorized with Azure
Active Directory (Azure AD). The default value is null, which is equivalent to true.</p>
</td>

StorageAccountProperties_AccessTier_STATUS
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AccessTier: Required for storage accounts where kind = BlobStorage. The access tier is used for billing. The &lsquo;Premium&rsquo;
access tier is the default value for premium block blobs storage account type and it cannot be changed for the premium
block blobs storage account type.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowBlobPublicAccess</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>

<p>AllowBlobPublicAccess: Allow or disallow public access to all blobs or containers in the storage account. The default
interpretation is true for this property.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowCrossTenantReplication</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>

for this property.</p>

</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowSharedKeyAccess</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowSharedKeyAccess: Indicates whether the storage account permits requests to be authorized with the account access
key via Shared Key. If false, then all requests, including shared access signatures, must be authorized with Azure
Active Directory (Azure AD). The default value is null, which is equivalent to true.</p>
</td>
</tr>

<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>

<tr>
<td>

<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_AccessTier">
StorageAccountPropertiesCreateParameters_AccessTier
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AccessTier: Required for storage accounts where kind = BlobStorage. The access tier is used for billing. The &lsquo;Premium&rsquo;
access tier is the default value for premium block blobs storage account type and it cannot be changed for the premium
block blobs storage account type.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowBlobPublicAccess</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>

interpretation is true for this property.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowCrossTenantReplication</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowCrossTenantReplication: Allow or disallow cross AAD tenant object replication. The default interpretation is true
for this property.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowSharedKeyAccess</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowSharedKeyAccess: Indicates whether the storage account permits requests to be authorized with the account access
key via Shared Key. If false, then all requests, including shared access signatures, must be authorized with Azure
Active Directory (Azure AD). The default value is null, which is equivalent to true.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>

</td>

doesn&rsquo;t have to be.</p>

<tr>
<td>
<code>customDomain</code><br/>
<em>

CustomDomain
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>CustomDomain: User domain assigned to the storage account. Name is the CNAME source. Only one custom domain is supported
per storage account at this time. To clear the existing custom domain, use an empty string for the custom domain name
property.</p>

map[string]string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Metadata: A name-value pair to associate with the share as metadata.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>owner</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="https://pkg.go.dev/github.com/Azure/azure-service-operator/v2/pkg/genruntime#KnownResourceReference">
genruntime.KnownResourceReference
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Owner: The owner of the resource. The owner controls where the resource goes when it is deployed. The owner also
controls the resources lifecycle. When the owner is deleted the resource will also be deleted. Owner is expected to be a
reference to a storage.azure.com/StorageAccountsFileService resource</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>rootSquash</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.FileShareProperties_RootSquash">
FileShareProperties_RootSquash
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>RootSquash: The property is for NFS share only. The default is NoRootSquash.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>shareQuota</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ShareQuota: The maximum size of the share, in gigabytes. Must be greater than 0, and less than or equal to 5TB (5120).
For Large File Shares, the maximum size is 102400.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>signedIdentifiers</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.SignedIdentifier">
[]SignedIdentifier
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>SignedIdentifiers: List of stored access policies specified on the share.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

</em>

Table service.</p>

<h3 id="storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.UpdateHistoryProperty_STATUS">UpdateHistoryProperty_STATUS
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#storage.azure.com/v1api20220901.ImmutabilityPolicyProperties_STATUS">ImmutabilityPolicyProperties_STATUS</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>An update history of the ImmutabilityPolicy of a blob container.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowProtectedAppendWrites</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowProtectedAppendWrites: This property can only be changed for unlocked time-based retention policies. When enabled,
new blocks can be written to an append blob while maintaining immutability protection and compliance. Only new blocks
can be added and any existing blocks cannot be modified or deleted. This property cannot be changed with
ExtendImmutabilityPolicy API.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>allowProtectedAppendWritesAll</code><br/>
<em>
bool
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>AllowProtectedAppendWritesAll: This property can only be changed for unlocked time-based retention policies. When
enabled, new blocks can be written to both &lsquo;Append and Bock Blobs&rsquo; while maintaining immutability protection and
compliance. Only new blocks can be added and any existing blocks cannot be modified or deleted. This property cannot be
changed with ExtendImmutabilityPolicy API. The &lsquo;allowProtectedAppendWrites&rsquo; and &lsquo;allowProtectedAppendWritesAll&rsquo;
properties are mutually exclusive.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>immutabilityPeriodSinceCreationInDays</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ImmutabilityPeriodSinceCreationInDays: The immutability period for the blobs in the container since the policy creation,
in days.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>objectIdentifier</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ObjectIdentifier: Returns the Object ID of the user who updated the ImmutabilityPolicy.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>tenantId</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>TenantId: Returns the Tenant ID that issued the token for the user who updated the ImmutabilityPolicy.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>timestamp</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>update</code><br/>

UpdateHistoryProperty_Update_STATUS
</a>
</em>
